country_event = {
	id = hellas.1
	title = hellas.1.t
	desc = hellas.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bloody_may_thess
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
    timeout_days = 4

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
			goto_province = 11818
            set_country_flag = GRE_strikes_dealt
            clr_country_flag = GRE_strikes_started
        }
    }
	
	#Give into Greece
	option = {
		name = hellas.1.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }

		GRE = {
            add_stability = 0.5
            add_war_support = 0.5
            activate_decision = political_stabilization
            add_days_remove  = {
                decision = political_stabilization
                days = 60
            }
            set_variable = { decision_taken = 0 }
            set_variable = { metaxas_pro_axis = 1 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
            if = {
                limit = { has_decision = workers_entering_factories }
                add_days_remove  = {
                    decision = workers_entering_factories
                    days = -30
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = axal_nl2_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = axal_h1_shift_axis_heavy_tt
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_dem_adverse = yes
            set_temp_com_catastrophic = yes
            set_temp_fas_favourable = yes
            set_temp_mon_favourable = yes
            #######################
            hidden_effect = { complete_national_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes }
            ######[REPORT EVENTS]######
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC1=60 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC2=61 }
            set_temp_variable = { CM=1 }
            set_temp_variable = { CD=2 }
            set_temp_variable = { CC=2 }
            set_temp_variable = { CF=1 }
            set_temp_variable = { b1=60 }
            set_temp_variable = { b2=40 }
            potentially_send_report_events_for_actions_tmpREAC1_tmpREAC2_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_and_code = yes
            custom_effect_tooltip = report_event_warning_potential_repercussions_diplomatic_tt
		}
    }
	option = {
		name = hellas.1.b

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
        }

		GRE = {
            add_stability = 0.25
            add_war_support = 0.25
            activate_decision = political_stabilization
            add_days_remove  = {
                decision = political_stabilization
                days = 150
            }
            set_variable = { decision_taken = 1 }
            set_variable = { metaxas_pro_axis = 0.5 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
            if = {
                limit = { has_decision = workers_entering_factories }
                add_days_remove  = {
                    decision = workers_entering_factories
                    days = -45
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = axal_nl2_tt
            custom_effect_tooltip = axal_h1_shift_axis_light_tt
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_dem_insignificant_negative = yes
            set_temp_com_slightly_detrimental = yes
            set_temp_fas_beneficial = yes
            set_temp_mon_beneficial = yes
            #######################
            hidden_effect = { complete_national_focus = GRE_escalating_strikes }
            ######[REPORT EVENTS]######
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC1=60 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC2=61 }
            set_temp_variable = { CM=1 }
            set_temp_variable = { CD=2 }
            set_temp_variable = { CC=2 }
            set_temp_variable = { CF=1 }
            set_temp_variable = { b1=90 }
            set_temp_variable = { b2=10 }
            potentially_send_report_events_for_actions_tmpREAC1_tmpREAC2_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_and_code = yes
            custom_effect_tooltip = report_event_warning_potential_repercussions_diplomatic_tt
		}
    }
	option = {
		name = hellas.1.c

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
        }

		GRE = {
            add_stability = -0.2
            add_war_support = -0.2

country_event = {
	id = hellas.2
	title = hellas.2.t
	desc = hellas.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_metaxas

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.2.a

        add_stability = 0.02
        add_war_support = 0.15
        swap_ruler_traits = { remove = greek_dictator add = arkhigos_0 }
        hidden_effect = { complete_national_focus = GRE_the_4th_of_august_regime }
        set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = "Kathestós tis 4hs Augoústou"
			name = "4h Augoústou"
		}
        set_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
        set_variable = { GRE_ark = 0 }
        if = { 
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 0 } } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_papagos_selection_tt
            #######################
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 0.10 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
            set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
            #########  ############
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_dem_adverse = yes
            set_temp_com_adverse = yes
            set_temp_fas_beneficial = yes
            set_temp_mon_favourable = yes 
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 1 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drakos_selection_tt            
            #######################
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 0.06 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
            set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_increase = 0.04 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }
            set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
            #########  ############
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_dem
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_com_catastrophic = yes
            set_temp_fas_insignificant_positive = yes
            set_temp_mon_favourable = yes
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 2 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_stanotas_selection_tt
            #######################
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 0.06 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
            set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_increase = 0.04 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }
            set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
            #########  ############
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_dem
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_dem_slightly_detrimental = yes
            set_temp_com_slightly_detrimental = yes
            set_temp_fas_insignificant_positive = yes
            set_temp_mon_slightly_beneficial = yes
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 3 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_zervas_selection_tt
            #######################
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_decrease = 0.05 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_decrease }
            set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_increase = 0.05 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }
            set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
            #########  ############
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_dem
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_mon
            ###FACTION MECHANICS###
            set_temp_dem_slightly_beneficial = yes
            set_temp_mon_slightly_detrimental = yes
            subtract_from_variable = { fct_mon = 2.5}   
            add_to_variable = { fct_dem = 2.5}
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon = -2.5}
            set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem = 2.5}
        }
        faction_gui_call = yes
        hidden_effect = { add_ideas=GRE_kostas_kotzias_political_advisor add_ideas=GRE_diakos }
    }    
}

country_event = {                                                       ### Archbishop
	id = hellas.5
	title = hellas.5.t
	desc = {
        text = hellas.5_a.desc
        trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.5_b.desc
        trigger = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_archbishop_election

	trigger = {
        has_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
        date > 1938.11.1
    }

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.5.a
        trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
        add_stability = 0.02
        set_country_flag = archbishop_chrysanthos_elected
        effect_tooltip = { activate_advisor = GRE_archbishop_chrysanthos_political_advisor }
        if = {
            limit = { amount_taken_ideas = { amount < 3 slots = { political_advisor } } }
            hidden_effect = { activate_advisor = GRE_archbishop_chrysanthos_political_advisor }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = activate_if_open_slot_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip =  hellas.5.a_tt
    } 
	option = {
		name = hellas.5.b

		ai_chance = {
            base = 0
        }
        if = { limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } add_stability = 0.1 add_political_power=50 }
        else = { add_stability = -0.05 }
        set_country_flag = archbishop_damaskinos_elected
        effect_tooltip = { activate_advisor = GRE_archbishop_damaskinos_political_advisor }
        if = {
            limit = { amount_taken_ideas = { amount < 3 slots = { political_advisor } } }
            hidden_effect = { activate_advisor = GRE_archbishop_damaskinos_political_advisor }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = activate_if_open_slot_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip =  hellas.5.b_tt
    }  
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.6
	title = hellas.6.t
	desc = hellas.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_red_dogs

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
        date > 1936.08.01
		tag = GRE
        OR = {
    		check_variable = { var = fct_com value = 40 compare = less_than }
            check_variable = { var = fct_dem value = 40 compare = less_than }
        }
        has_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days=7 }
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {   
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = fct_com value = 40 compare = less_than } } set_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1  }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { var = fct_dem value = 40 compare = less_than } } set_country_flag = GRE_repub_upr_1 }
        }
    }

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.6.a
        add_stability = -0.05
    }
}

country_event = {               #IMRO GETS THE BOOT BY HAVING THE SLAVS CRUSHED (METAXAS DECISION)
	id = hellas.9
	title = hellas.9.t
	desc = hellas.9.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_greek_march

	trigger = {
		tag = GRE
        has_country_flag = BUL_imro_awakened_in_country_flag
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.9.a
        set_country_flag = BUL_repress_imro_flag
        clr_country_flag = BUL_repress_imro_flag
        clr_country_flag = BUL_imro_awakened_in_country_flag
        add_political_power = 150
        BUL = { add_political_power = -150 }
        every_controlled_state = { 
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = skirmishes_against_imro }
                }
            remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = skirmishes_against_imro }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = widespread_bulgarian_sentiment_01 }
                }
                remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = widespread_bulgarian_sentiment_01 }
            }
            remove_core_of = BUL
            add_core_of = ROOT
        }     
    }    
}


unit_leader_event = {               # 1 / 8 / 1936 -> Papagos becomes FeldMarshall.
	id = hellas.11
	title = hellas.11.t
	desc = { 
        text = hellas.11.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { decision_taken < 1 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.11.desc2
        trigger = { check_variable = { decision_taken > 0 } }
    }
    
    is_triggered_only = yes 
    timeout_days = 6
    option = {
        ai_chance = { base=100 }
        name = hellas.11.a
        GRE_alexandros_papagos = { promote_leader=yes promote_officer=yes if={ limit={NOT={has_trait=gre_recently_trained_general}} reduce_unpreparedness = yes }}
        hidden_effect = { activate_advisor = GRE_alexandros_papagos_chief }
        custom_effect_tooltip = axal_nl2_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_papagos_selection_event_tt
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.11.b
        trigger = { check_variable= { GRE.decision_taken > 0 }}
        GRE_markos_drakos = { promote_leader=yes promote_officer=yes if={ limit={NOT={has_trait=gre_recently_trained_general}} reduce_unpreparedness = yes }}
        hidden_effect = { activate_advisor = GRE_markos_drakos_chief }
        set_variable = { GRE.decision_taken = 1 }
        custom_effect_tooltip = axal_nl2_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drakos_selection_event_tt
    }
    option = {
        name = hellas.11.c
        trigger = { check_variable={ GRE.decision_taken > 0 }}
        GRE_georgios_stanotas = { promote_leader=yes promote_officer=yes if={ limit={NOT={has_trait=gre_recently_trained_general}} reduce_unpreparedness = yes }}
        hidden_effect = { activate_advisor = GRE_georgios_stanotas_chief }
        set_variable = { GRE.decision_taken = 2 }
        custom_effect_tooltip = axal_nl2_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_stanotas_selection_event_tt
    }
    option = {

country_event = {
	id = hellas.17
	title = hellas.17.t
	desc = hellas.17.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_monarchists_power_up

	trigger = { 
        original_tag = GRE
        check_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier < 4 }
        has_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
        has_country_flag = GRE_faction_gui_flag
        NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 120
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { tmp = 1 }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.final_mon_military_weight = 0 } } set_temp_variable = { mg = 0.005 } }
            else = { set_temp_variable = { mg = GRE.final_mon_military_weight } multiply_temp_variable = { mg = 0.04 } }
            divide_temp_variable = { tmp = mg }
            factor = tmp
            always = yes
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.17.a
        set_temp_variable_to_random = { var = tmp_mon_effect_increase min = 0.04 max = 0.06}
        #set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 0.05 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_over_200_danger_tt
        GRE_faction_mon_refresh = yes
    }
}

	id = hellas.202

	desc = hellas.202.desc

        mussolini_historical_tensions_with_greece = yes
        annexation_of_albania_has_occurred_one_way_or_another = yes
        set_temp_variable = { x = ITA.army_intel@GRE }                              ### FORMULA: y = -0.25x + 30 where y the num of divisions and x the army intel italy has over greece (5,30 min-max)
        multiply_temp_variable = { x = -0.25 }
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = 30 }
        num_divisions > x
		date > 1936.08.04
        has_country_leader = {
            name = "Ioannis Metaxas"
            ruling_only = yes
        }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
    
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.202.a
        activate_mission = GRE_activated_mission_2
    }

	trigger = {

        set_temp_variable = { x = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
        check_variable = { x > eq_thr?10000 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
    
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { evnt_cnt_203 = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { eq_thr?10000 = 5000 }
        }
    }
    
	option = {
		name = hellas.203.a
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { evnt_cnt_203 = 1 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_25_percent_of_lvl3_generals_tt
        }
        else = {
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_percent_in_order_generals_tt
        }
        hidden_effect = { activate_decision = hidden_proc_for_equip_event }
    }      
}

		name = hellas.223.a
        set_temp_variable = { indX = GRE.army_leaders } set_temp_variable = { indY = 0.20 } multiply_temp_variable = { indX = indY } 
        custom_effect_tooltip = train_random_percentage_tt
        hidden_effect = { activate_decision = hidden_proc_for_support_event }
    }
}

state_event = {                                                                        # Mining Rights Events
	id = hellas.241
	title = hellas.241.t
	desc = hellas.241.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_bank_of_greece
	is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ###[State Temp Variables]###
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_oil = resource@oil }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_aluminium = resource@aluminium }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_rubber = resource@rubber }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_tungsten = resource@tungsten }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_steel = resource@steel }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_chromium = resource@chromium }
            set_variable = { GRE.h241_state_id = THIS.id}
            every_country = {
                limit = { is_influencable=yes is_major=yes num_of_military_factories>20 num_of_civilian_factories>20 has_capitulated=no }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_oil > 0 } }
                    ###[Oil]###
                    if = { limit = { OR = { original_tag = GER original_tag = JAP original_tag = ITA } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.25 } }
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@oil }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@oil }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { fuel_available = produces }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                check_variable = { fuel_available < 75 }
                                fuel_ratio < 0.41
                            }
                        }
                        multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.25 }
                    }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_aluminium > 0 } }
                    ###[Aluminium]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@aluminium }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@aluminium }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { aluminium_available = produces }                          ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { aluminium_required = THIS.resource_consumed@aluminium }   ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { aluminium_required > aluminium_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_rubber > 0 } }
                    ###[Rubber]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@rubber }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@rubber }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { rubber_available = produces }                             ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { rubber_required = THIS.resource_consumed@rubber }         ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { rubber_required > rubber_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_tungsten > 0 } }
                    ###[Tungsten]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@tungsten }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@tungsten }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { tungsten_available = produces }                           ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { tungsten_required = THIS.resource_consumed@tungsten }     ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { tungsten_required > tungsten_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_steel > 0 } }
                    ###[Steel]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@steel }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@steel }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { steel_available = produces }                              ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { steel_required = THIS.resource_consumed@steel }           ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { steel_required > steel_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.h241_state_chromium > 0 } }
                    ###[Chromium]###
                    set_temp_variable = { produces = THIS.resource_produced@chromium }
                    set_temp_variable = { exports = THIS.resource_exported@chromium }
                    subtract_from_temp_variable = { produces = exports }
                    set_temp_variable = { chromium_available = produces }                           ## Available Resource
                    set_temp_variable = { chromium_required = THIS.resource_consumed@chromium }     ## Requirements
                    if = { limit = { check_variable = { chromium_required > chromium_available } } multiply_variable = { h241_needed_weight?1 = 1.1 } }
                }
                add_to_array = { GRE.h241_id = THIS.id }
                add_to_array = { GRE.h241_weight = h241_needed_weight }
                clear_variable = h241_needed_weight
            }
        }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.241.a
        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.242 days = 0 } }
    }
}

country_event = {               #MINING RIGHTS - RETURN EVENT
	id = hellas.242
	title = hellas.242.t
	desc = hellas.242.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_variable = { iterations = h241_id^num }
            while_loop_effect = {
                break = br
                limit = { always = yes }
                
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { h241_id^num = 0 } } set_temp_variable = { br = 1 } }
                else = {
                    find_highest_in_array = { array = h241_weight value = val_highest index = idx_highest }
                    add_to_array = { h241_sorted_weight = val_highest }
                    add_to_array = { h241_sorted_id = h241_id^idx_highest }
                    remove_from_array = { array = h241_weight index = idx_highest }
                    remove_from_array = { array = h241_id index = idx_highest }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^0 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^0 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^0 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^1 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^1 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^1 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^2 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^2 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^2 }

        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.e
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^3 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^3 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^3 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.f
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^4 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^4 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^4 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.g
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^5 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^5 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^5 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.h
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^6 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^6 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^6 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.i
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_sorted_weight^7 > 0 } }
        set_variable = { h241_return_id = h241_sorted_id^7 }
        set_variable = { h241_return_weight = h241_sorted_weight^7 }
        country_event = { id = hellas.243 days = 0 }
        clear_array = h241_sorted_id
        clear_array = h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array = h241_weight
        clear_array = h241_id
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.242.j
        h241_clear_variables = yes

country_event = {               #MINING RIGHTS - FINAL PART A
	id = hellas.243
	title = hellas.243.t
	desc = hellas.243.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        if = { limit = { check_variable = { h241_first_run = 0 } }
            hidden_effect = {
                ##################################[ State Calculators ]######################################
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_oil}                      # price = 0.2 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.2 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_aluminium}                # price = 0.08 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.08 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_rubber}                   # price = 0.18 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.18 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_tungsten}                 # price = 0.13 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.13 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_steel}                    # price = 0.10 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.1 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp = GRE.h241_state_chromium}                 # price = 0.07 * x
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = 0.07 }
                add_to_variable = { total_worth = tmp }
                multiply_variable = { total_worth = h241_return_weight }
                round_variable = total_worth
                set_variable = { dec_pp_gain = 50 }
                multiply_variable = { dec_pp_gain = total_worth }
                set_variable = { dec_inf_equipment = total_worth }
                multiply_variable = { dec_inf_equipment = 500 }
                set_variable = { dec_art_equipment = total_worth }
                multiply_variable = { dec_art_equipment = 42 }
                set_variable = { dec_sup_equipment = total_worth }
                multiply_variable = { dec_sup_equipment = 45 }
                set_variable = { dec_factories_worth = total_worth }
                ##################################[ Recipient Willingness ]######################################
                set_variable = { h241_willingness = 1 }
                set_variable = { tmp_favor_multiplier = 1}
                random_country = {
                    limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                    set_temp_variable = { x = THIS.favor@GRE }
                }
                divide_temp_variable = { x = 100 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 1 }
                multiply_variable = { h241_willingness = x }
                calculate_alax_multiplier = yes
                multiply_variable = { h241_willingness = alax_multiplier }
                #################################################################################################
                add_to_variable = { h241_first_run = 1 }
            }
        }
    }

    #1. Political Power
    #2. Influence   ~Requires still influencable~
    #3. Equipment ~Requires not at war or at required in stockpile~
    #4. Diplomatic Support ~later on~
    #5. Country Specific Favors

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_pp_chosen = 0 } }
        effect_tooltip = { add_political_power = dec_pp_gain }
        set_variable = { dec_pp_chosen = 1 }
        #####################[Calculate Willingness Effects]############################
        random_country = {
            limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
            set_temp_variable = { x = political_power }
            set_temp_variable = { y = political_power_daily}
        }
        set_temp_variable = { z = dec_pp_gain }
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 2 }                # 50% of pp for check
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { x > z } }
            set_variable = { pp_willingness_cost = 0.5 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                multiply_temp_variable = { y = 180 }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { z = y }
                check_variable = { x > z }
            }
            set_variable = { pp_willingness_cost = 0.65 }
        }
        else = { set_variable = { pp_willingness_cost = 1.0 } }
        subtract_from_variable = { h241_willingness = pp_willingness_cost }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_pp_chosen > 0 } }
        add_to_variable = { h241_willingness = pp_willingness_cost }
        clear_variable = dec_pp_chosen
        clear_variable = pp_willingness_cost
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen = 0 } }
        effect_tooltip = {
            random_country = {
                limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = infantry_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_inf_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = support_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_sup_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = artillery_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_art_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
            }
        }
        set_variable = { dec_equip_chosen = 1 }
        #####################[Calculate Willingness Effects]############################
        random_country = {
            limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
            set_temp_variable = { x1 = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
            set_temp_variable = { x2 = num_equipment@support_equipment }
            set_temp_variable = { x3 = num_equipment@artillery_equipment }
            set_temp_variable = { y1 = num_of_civilian_factories }
            set_temp_variable = { y2 = num_of_military_factories }          # base 4.5
            set_temp_variable = { y3 = num_of_factories }
        }
        set_temp_variable = { z = dec_inf_equipment }           # Take the guns
        divide_temp_variable = { z = y2 }                       # Divide by number of factories
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 0.5 }                      # Divide by 2 to simulate half Mils taken (not 100%)
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 180 }                      # Divide by number of days they will gain rights. We got cost/day.
        divide_temp_variable = { z = 4.5 }                      # Divide by 4.5 to gain x.xxx based percentage of factory capabilities
        if = {
            limit = { has_war = yes OR = { check_variable = { x1 < 1 } check_variable = { x2 < 1 } check_variable = { x3 < 1 } } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 5 }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_war = no check_variable = { x1 < 1 } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 2.5 }
            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_war = no check_variable = { x1 > 0 } check_variable = { x1 < var:dec_inf_equipment } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 2.0 }
            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_war = no NOT = { check_variable = { x1 < var:dec_inf_equipment } } }
            set_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = 1.25 }
            multiply_variable = { eq_willingness_cost = z }
        }
        subtract_from_variable = { h241_willingness = eq_willingness_cost }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.d
        trigger = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen > 0 } }
        clear_variable = dec_equip_chosen
        add_to_variable = { h241_willingness = eq_willingness_cost }
        clear_variable = eq_willingness_cost
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.244 days = 0 } } }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.e
        h241_clear_variables = yes
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.243.f
        country_event = { id = hellas.245 days = 0 }
    }
}

	id = hellas.245
	title = hellas.245.t
	desc = hellas.245.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no


    option = {                                                  ## Accepted
        trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { h241_willingness < 0 } } }
        name = hellas.245.a
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { dec_pp_chosen > 0 } }
            add_political_power = var:dec_pp_gain
            set_temp_variable = { x = var:dec_pp_gain }
            multiply_temp_variable = { x = -1 }
            random_country = {
                limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                add_political_power = x
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { dec_equip_chosen > 0 } }
            random_country = {
                limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = infantry_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_inf_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = support_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_sup_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
                send_equipment = {
                    equipment = artillery_equipment
                    amount = var:GRE.dec_art_equipment
                    target = GRE
                }
            }
        }
        random_country = {
            limit = { tag = var:GRE.h241_return_id }
            GRE = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = PREV state = var:GRE.h241_state_id } }
        }
        hidden_effect = {
            random_state = {
                limit = { state = var:GRE.h241_state_id }
                set_state_flag = given_mining_rights
                set_variable = { return_owner = GRE.h241_return_id }
            }
            h241_clear_variables = yes
        }
    }

    option = {                                                  ## Rejected
        trigger = { check_variable = { h241_willingness < 0 } }
        name = hellas.245.b
        h241_clear_variables = yes
    }
}

country_event = {               #BRITISH RESPONSE
	id = hellas.3095
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_a trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 1 } } }
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_b trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 2 } } }
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_c trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 3 } } }
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_d trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 4 } } }
	desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_a trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 1 } } }
    desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_b trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 2 } } }
    desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_c trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 3 } } }
    desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_d trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 4 } } }
    picture = GFX_report_event_belgrade_1939

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ###[British Influence]###
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-60 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 90 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-60 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-30 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 5 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 15 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 80 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=0 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 5 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 15 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 70 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=0 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=30 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 40 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=40 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 20 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 20 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=50 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 25 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 50 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 15 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=50 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=60 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 35 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 50 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 5 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=70 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=80 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 50 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 40 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=80 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=90 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 60 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=90 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=95 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 80 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=95 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=100 compare=less_than_or_equals }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 100 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            ###[AXAL]###
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 5 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 100 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 10 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 75 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 20 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 70 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 30 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 40 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 40.01 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 30 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 59.99 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 25 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 70 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 80 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 40 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 90 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 70 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 95.01 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 75 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 } }
            else = { add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 100 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 } }
            ###[BASE BIAS]###
            add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 30 } 
            add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } 
            add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } 
            add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 }
            ###[AVERAGE]###
            divide_temp_variable = { b1 = 3 }
            divide_temp_variable = { b2 = 3 }
            divide_temp_variable = { b3 = 3 }
            divide_temp_variable = { b4 = 3 }
            ###[PROTEST LEVEL ADJUSTMENTS]###
            if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { GRE.protest_level = 4 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 2.00 }   #100%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 1.50 }   #50%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.50 }   #50%lower
                multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.10 }   #90%lower
                log="DID IT"
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { GRE.protest_level = 3 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 1.75 }   #75%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 1.25 }   #25%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.75 }   #25%lower
                multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.25 }   #75%lower
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { GRE.protest_level = 2 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 1.50 }   #50%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 1.25 }   #25%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.75 }   #25%lower
                multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.50 }   #50%lower
            }
            log="[?b1]"
            log="[?b2]"
            log="[?b3]"
            log="[?b4]"
            ###[FINAL]###
            random_list = {
                seed = random
                var:b1 = { set_variable = { opt = 1 } }
                var:b2 = { set_variable = { opt = 2 } }
                var:b3 = { set_variable = { opt = 3 } }
                var:b4 = { set_variable = { opt = 4 } }
            }
        }
    }
	
	option = { # Best Result
		name = hellas.3095.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 1 } }
        add_political_power = 150
        add_stability = 0.1
        add_war_support = 0.1
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag=balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = 75
            add_stability = 0.05
            add_war_support = 0.05
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=1.50 } 
            add_to_variable = { overall_alliance_weight=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_increased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = 5 }
        add_to_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE = findY }
        custom_effect_tooltip = favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }
    option = { # 2nd Best Result
		name = hellas.3095.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 2 } }
        add_political_power = 75
        add_stability = 0.05
        add_war_support = 0.05
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = 25
            add_stability = 0.02
            add_war_support = 0.02
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=0.75 } 
            add_to_variable = { overall_alliance_weight=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_increased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = 5 }
        add_to_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE = findY }
        custom_effect_tooltip = favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }  
    option = { # 2nd Worst Result
		name = hellas.3095.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 3 } }
        add_political_power = -75
        add_stability = -0.05
        add_war_support = -0.05
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = -25
            add_stability = -0.02
            add_war_support = -0.02
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=-0.75 } 
            add_to_variable = { overall_alliance_weight=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_decreased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
        add_to_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE = findY }
        custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }
    option = { # Worst Result
		name = hellas.3095.d
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 4 } }
        add_political_power = -150
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_war_support = -0.1
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = -75
            add_stability = -0.05
            add_war_support = -0.05
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=-1.50 } 
            add_to_variable = { overall_alliance_weight=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_decreased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
        add_to_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE = findY }
        custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }
}

country_event = {               #THE PRO-AXIS PLOT
	id = hellas.317
	title = hellas.317.t
	desc = {                                                                                        ## Greece was denied by the Germans
        text = hellas.317.desc
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot
            has_country_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal
        }
    }
    picture = GFX_report_event_1940_plot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_country_flag = GRE_plot_occurred
        }
    }
	
	option = {                                      ## Went in prepared
		name = hellas.317.a
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot
            GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal }
        }
        add_political_power = 400
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 0.25 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
    }  

    option = {                                      ## Went in partially unprepared
		name = hellas.317.b
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                AND = {
                    has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot
                    NOT = { GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal } }
                }
                AND = {
                    has_country_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal
                    NOT = { GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal } }
                }
            }
        }
        add_political_power = -100
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_war_support = -0.05
    } 
    
    option = {                                      ## Went in completely unprepared
		name = hellas.317.c
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot }
            NOT = { GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal } }
        }
        add_political_power = -400
        add_stability = -0.4
        add_war_support = -0.2
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = -0.25 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
    } 
}

	desc = hellas.3200.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {                                                                                              ### Bulgaria accepts
		name = hellas.3200.a    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
        BUL = {
            clr_country_flag = channels_established
            set_country_flag = common_strategy_with_greece_defined 
            add_opinion_modifier = { 
                target = GRE
                modifier = GRE_common_balkan_strategy
            }
            hidden_effect = {
                remove_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = GRE
                    modifier = BFTB_incongruous_neighbors
                }
                remove_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROM
                    modifier = BFTB_incongruous_neighbors
                }
                remove_opinion_modifier = {

			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
        GRE = { add_political_power = 300 }
        add_political_power = 75
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = guarantee
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        GRE = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = ENG
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            } 
        }
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = docking_rights
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        GRE = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = ENG
                relation = docking_rights
                active = yes
            }  
        }
        ### THE FOLLOWING BLOCK ADDS A MASSIVE BOOST OF FAVOR TO UK AND THEIR ALLIES. LIKEWISE SUBTRACTS A MASSIVE AMOUNT OF FAVOR FROM THEIR ENEMIES.
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = {
                        array = global.favor_mechanic
                        value = THIS.id
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            is_in_faction_with = ENG
                            AND = {
                                original_tag = USA
                                has_government = democratic
                                ENG = { has_government = democratic }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 30 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            original_tag = GER
                            original_tag = ITA
                            original_tag = BUL
                        }
                        NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            original_tag = GER
                        }
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 20 } 
                    }
                    else = {
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 30 }   
                    } 
                }
            } 
        }
        news_event = { id = hellenic_news.200 days = 0 }
    }  
	option = {  ### BRITAIN DECLINES
		name = hellas.3182.b    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
			}
		}        
        GRE = { add_political_power = 150 }  
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {

                        value = THIS.id

country_event = {                                       # REACTION TO ACTION EVENT (#1)
	id = hellas.3320001
	title = hellas.332.t
    desc = "[GetEvent332Desc]"
    picture = "[GetEvent332Picture]"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ###[Set & Reset]###
            set_temp_variable = { TYPE=FROM.e332_1_t@GRE }
            set_temp_variable = { MAG=FROM.e332_1_MAG@GRE }
            for_each_loop = { array=FROM.e332_1_ARRVAL@GRE add_to_temp_array={ARRVAL=v }}
            ###[Effects]###

        }
    }
	
	option = {
        name=hellas.332.a
        if = {
            limit = {check_variable={ FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=50 }}
            set_temp_variable = { findX=FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY=-5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE=findY }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { OR={ check_variable={ FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=60 } check_variable={FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=62 }}}
            set_temp_variable = { findX=FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=0.25 max=3 integer=no }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_boost_with_findX_by_findY
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE=findY }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { OR={ check_variable={ FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=61 } check_variable={FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=63 }}}
            set_temp_variable = { findX=FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=-3 max=-0.25 integer=no }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE=findY }
        }
        ###[Clear FROM from Array]###
        remove_from_array = { GRE.e_332_1 = FROM.id }
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_1_t@GRE
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_1_MAG@GRE
        clear_array    = FROM.e332_1_ARRVAL@GRE
    }
    option = {
        name=hellas.332.r52_1
        trigger = { check_variable={ FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=52 }}
        set_temp_variable = { quantity=FROM.e332_1_MAG@GRE }
        multiply_temp_variable = { quantity=-50 }
        add_political_power = quantity
        ###[Clear FROM from Array]###
        remove_from_array = { GRE.e_332_1 = FROM.id }
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_1_t@GRE
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_1_MAG@GRE
        clear_array    = FROM.e332_1_ARRVAL@GRE
    }
    option = {
        name=hellas.332.r52_2
        trigger = { check_variable={ FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=52 }}
        ###[Clear FROM from Array]###
        remove_from_array = { GRE.e_332_1 = FROM.id }
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_1_t@GRE
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_1_MAG@GRE
        clear_array    = FROM.e332_1_ARRVAL@GRE
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.350
	title = hellas.350.t
	desc = hellas.350.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_maniadakis_rounding_up

	trigger = {
        has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr
        NOT = { has_country_flag = com_civilwar_started }
        check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr < 120 }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 160
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { cnt = amount_of_work_in_asfaleia }
            set_temp_variable = { final = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { weight = 0.05 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { weight = cnt }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { final = weight }
            factor = final
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr < 181 }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.25
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr > 180 }
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.350.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }
        add_days_mission_timeout = {
            mission = GRE_comm_upr
            days = 30
        }
    }  
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.352
	title = hellas.352.t
	desc = hellas.352.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_republicans_rebellious

	trigger = {
        original_tag = GRE
        has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr
        NOT = { has_country_flag = republican_uprising_utterly_crushed }
        NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }
        check_variable = { fct_dem < 40 }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 240
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { x = fct_dem }
            divide_temp_variable = { x = 40 }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { fct_dem < 20 } } divide_temp_variable = { x = 2 } }
            factor = x
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
    timeout_days = 5
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.352.a

		ai_chance = {base = 100}
        ###[Increase Overall Effect Multiplier]###
        set_temp_variable_to_random = { var = tmp_dem_effect_increase min = 0.06 max = 0.14 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_dem
        ###[Remove Days from Mission]###
        set_temp_variable = { current_remaining = days_mission_timeout@GRE_repub_upr }
        set_temp_variable_to_random =  { var = percentage_days_lost min = 0.01 max = 0.2 }
        multiply_temp_variable = { current_remaining = percentage_days_lost }
        multiply_temp_variable = { current_remaining = -1 }
        add_days_mission_timeout = {
            mission = GRE_repub_upr
            days = current_remaining
        }
        ################################
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_over_200_danger_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip = h352_dem_additional_days_lost_tt
        GRE_faction_refresh = yes
    }
}

	desc = hellas.353.desc

        original_tag = GRE
        NOT = { has_country_flag = communist_uprising_utterly_crushed }
        has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr

    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {

    timeout_days = 5

		name = hellas.353.a

        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = tmp_com_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_com_effect_multiplier = tmp_com_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_com
        ###[Remove Days from Mission]###
        set_temp_variable = { current_remaining = days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr }
        set_temp_variable_to_random =  { var = percentage_days_lost min = 0.01 max = 0.2 }

        multiply_temp_variable = { current_remaining = -1 }
        add_days_mission_timeout = {
            mission = GRE_comm_upr
            days = current_remaining

	desc = hellas.354.desc

        original_tag = GRE

            AND = {
                NOT = { has_government = neutrality }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = mon_civilwar_started }

                check_variable = { fct_mon < 20 }
            }
            AND = {
                has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr

                NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }

                has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr

country_event = {       ## Choose Partner to Modernize the army
	id = hellas.405
	title = hellas.405.t
	desc = hellas.405.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hold_on

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {  ##ENG/FRA
		name = hellas.405.a
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = FRA.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
        }     
        #hidden_effect = {
            ### MOTORIZED / MECH1 ###
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = motorised_infantry } }
                set_technology = { motorised_infantry = 1 }
            }
            ########################
            ###       TANKS      ###
            set_technology = { gwtank_chassis = 1 }
            if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank_chassis } OR = { ENG = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank_chassis } FRA = { has_tech = basic_heavy_tank_chassis } } } add_tech_bonus = { bonus = 3.0 uses = 1 category = cat_heavy_armor } }
            else_if = { limit = { NOT = { has_tech = basic_medium_tank_chassis } OR = { ENG = { has_tech = basic_medium_tank_chassis } FRA = { has_tech = basic_medium_tank_chassis } } } add_tech_bonus = { bonus = 3.0 uses = 1 category = cat_medium_armor } }

                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = bicycle_infantry } JAP = { has_tech = bicycle_infantry } }
                set_technology = { bicycle_infantry = 1 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = armored_car1 } JAP = { has_tech = armored_car1 } }

            if = {

                set_technology = { armor_tech_1 = 1 }
            }

                    JAP = { has_tech = armor_tech_1 }
                }
                set_technology = { engine_tech_1 = 1 }
            }
            ########################
            ###      SUPPORT     ###

            set_temp_variable = { limit = 3 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = support_picked_in_order_tt

                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_engineers2 } JAP = { has_tech = tech_engineers2 } check_variable = { x < limit }  }
                set_technology = { tech_engineers2 = 1 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x = 1 }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_recon2 } JAP = { has_tech = tech_recon2 } check_variable = { x < limit }  }
                set_technology = { tech_recon2 = 1 }

            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_maintenance_company } JAP = { has_tech = tech_maintenance_company }  }
                set_technology = { tech_maintenance_company = 1 }
            }
            if = {

                set_technology = { tech_maintenance_company2 = 1 }

            }
            if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_tech = tech_field_hospital } JAP = { has_tech = tech_field_hospital }  }
                set_technology = { tech_field_hospital = 1 }
            }
            if = {

                set_technology = { tech_field_hospital2 = 1 }

            }

    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.407_negative.desc

    }

        }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.500
	title = hellas.500.t
	desc = hellas.500.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.500.a #small investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 30 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.75
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 40 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.5
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 70 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 4
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 70 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 8
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 14
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 20
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GRE_small_investment
			days = 30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GRE = {
				country_event = { id = hellas.501 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = hellas.500.b #no investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		GRE = { 
			country_event = { id = hellas.502 days = 2 }
		}
	}	
}
