country_event = {                                                                           ### - Mediocre Investment
	id = hellas.503
	title = hellas.503.t
	desc = hellas.503.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
    
	option = {
		name = hellas.503.a #medium investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 30 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.75
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 40 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 1.5
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 2
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 70 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 4
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 70 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 8
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 14
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 90 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = less_than }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 20
                check_variable = { var = THIS.favor@GRE value = 95 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            }
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = GRE_moderate_investment
			days = 30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GRE = {
				country_event = { id = hellas.504 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = hellas.503.b #no investment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		GRE = { 
			country_event = { id = hellas.502 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}


### -> Expand Mines (limited times, offers an influence boost)
### -> Substantial building slot expansion, additionally 1+1 factory.
### -> Oil drilling (ONCE - country chosen gets influence boost)
### -> Outsourcing (grants off-map factories but cancels when at war or allied with opponents)

country_event = {                                                                           ### - Greece receives mediocre Investment
	id = hellas.504
	title = hellas.504.t
	desc = hellas.504.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
    
	option = {                                                                                  ### Opening up the Land
		name = hellas.504.a #medium investment
        if = {                                                                              
            limit = {
                FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = ENG
                        original_tag = USA
                        original_tag = FRA
                    }
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_extra_slots_per_manpower_better_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                every_owned_state = {   
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 400
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 800
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    } 
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 1200
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
                    }   
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 2000
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
                    }  
                    else = {
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 5
                    }            
                }
            }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -6.5 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 6.5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
        else = {
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_extra_slots_per_manpower_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                every_owned_state = {   
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 400
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 0
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 800
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
                    } 
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 1200
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
                    }   
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            state_population_k < 2000
                        }
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
                    }  
                    else = {
                        add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
                    }            
                }    
            }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
    }
	option = {                                                                                  ### Outsourcing -> Leads to event below
		name = hellas.504.b #medium investment
        trigger = { 
            factories_within_investment_limit_FROM_to_GRE = yes
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_outsourcing_tt
        country_event = { id = hellas.505 days = 0 }
    }
    
	option = {                                                                                  ### Oil Drilling
		name = hellas.504.c #medium investment
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE_drilled_for_oil value = 0 compare = equals }
        }
        if = {                                                                              
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_drilled_for_oil value = 0 compare = equals }
                FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = SOV
                        original_tag = USA
                    }
                }
            }
            187 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = oil
                    amount = 12
                }
            } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drilling_for_oil_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_drilled_for_oil = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -10 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 10 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_drilled_for_oil value = 0 compare = equals }
            }
            187 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = oil
                    amount = 8
                }
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drilling_for_oil_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_drilled_for_oil = 1 }  
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -8 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 8 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
    }
	option = {                                                                                  ### Expand Mines
		name = hellas.504.d #medium investment
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 2 compare = less_than_or_equals }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 0 compare = equals }
            }
            186 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 3
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = chromium
                    amount = 8
                }
            }
            47 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 4
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = tungsten
                    amount = 2
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_mine_expansion = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 1 compare = equals }
            }
            186 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 3
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = chromium
                    amount = 4
                }
            }
            47 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 2
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = tungsten
                    amount = 4
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_mine_expansion = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = { var = GRE_mine_expansion value = 2 compare = equals }
            }
            186 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 6
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = chromium
                    amount = 8
                }
            }
            47 = { 
                add_resource = { 
                    type = steel
                    amount = 6
                }
                add_resource = { 
                    type = tungsten
                    amount = 4
                }
            }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_favor_boost_mediocre_from_tt
            add_to_variable = { GRE_mine_expansion = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.favor@GRE = 5 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }        
    }  
    option = {                                                                                  ### Go Back
		name = hellas.504.e

        add_political_power = 125
    }

            set_temp_variable = { findY = -6 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.FROM.favor@GRE = 6 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
    }
    option = {                                                                                  ### Docs
		name = hellas.505.c
        if = {
            limit = {
                FROM.FROM = {
                    OR = {
                        original_tag = ENG
                        original_tag = USA
                    }
                }
            }
            add_offsite_building = { type = dockyard level = 2 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.dockslent@GRE = 2 }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -8 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.FROM.favor@GRE = 8 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
        else = {
            add_offsite_building = { type = dockyard level = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { FROM.FROM.dockslent@GRE = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -6 }
            subtract_from_variable = { FROM.FROM.favor@GRE = 6 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = favor_hit_with_findX_by_findY
        }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                               ### Turkish Stance
	id = hellas.94
	title = hellas.94.t
	desc = {
        text = hellas.94_alliance.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { result = 2 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.94_positive.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { result = 1 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.94_neutral.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { result = 0 } }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_ismet_inonu

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ############[ Turkish Related ]############
            if = {
                limit = { has_fully_realized_the_balkan_pact=yes }
                set_temp_variable = { alliance_chance = 100 }
                set_temp_variable = { positive_chance = 0 }
                set_temp_variable = { neutral_chance = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_enacted_alliance_with_turkey=yes }
                set_temp_variable = { alliance_chance = TUR.overall_alliance_weight }
                multiply_temp_variable = { alliance_chance = 10 }
                set_temp_variable = { positive_chance = 100 }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { positive_chance = alliance_chance }
                set_temp_variable = { alliance_chance = 0 }
            }
            else = {
                set_temp_variable = { positive_chance = TUR.overall_alliance_weight }
                multiply_temp_variable = { positive_chance = 10 }
                set_temp_variable = { neutral_chance = 100 }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { neutral_chance = positive_chance }
                set_temp_variable = { alliance_chance = 0 }
            }
            random_list = {
                log = yes
                seed = random
                var:alliance_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = 2 } }
                var:positive_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = 1 } }
                var:neutral_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = 0 } }
            }
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { result > 0 } }
                GRE = { complete_national_focus = GRE_turkic_guarantees_against_bulgarians }
            }
            set_variable = { TUR.grecoitalian_stance=result }
        }
    }

    is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { name = hellas.94.a }
}

                set_temp_variable = { positive_chance = 0 }

                log = yes
                seed = random
                var:alliance_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = 2 } }
                var:positive_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = 1 } }
                var:neutral_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = 0 } }
                var:betrayal_chance = { set_temp_variable = { result = -1 } }

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Approach the Germans 
	id = hellas.109
	title = hellas.109.t
	desc = hellas.109.desc
	#picture = GFX_report_event_germany_politician_handshake

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {                                                                                      ## Germans Accept -> Toss the ball to the Italians 
		name = hellas.109.a
        
        ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 10
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
		}
        
        hidden_effect = {
            ITA = { country_event = { id = hellas.110 days = 0 }  }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Germans Decline (/continue war)
		name = hellas.109.b
        
        ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {

                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
		}
        
        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.112 days = 0 }  } 
    }

		name = hellas.110.a

			base = 1
            modifier = {
                factor = 5
                check_variable = { var = ITA.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = ITA.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
            }
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				check_variable = { var = ITA.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 1000
                GRE = { has_collaboration = { target = ITA value > 0.5} }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 20
                check_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown > 0 }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 5
                date < 1941.1.1
            }
		}
        
        hidden_effect = {
            GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.111 days = 0 }  }                                 
        }
    }

			base = 10
		}

    }

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Greece managed to capilutate Bulgaria on time 
	id = hellas.113
	title = hellas.113.t
	desc = hellas.113.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bulgarslayer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                                      ## Annex if collaborative  
		name = hellas.113.a
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.45}
        }
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 3 }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.75}
            }
            annex_country = {
                target = BUL
                transfer_troops = yes
            }            
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.45}
            }
            annex_country = {
                target = BUL
                transfer_troops = no
            }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Make it integrated puppet
		name = hellas.113.b
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0}
            }
        }
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 2 }
        hidden_effect = {
            puppet = BUL
            set_autonomy = {
                target = BUL
                autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
            }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Keep as it is
		name = hellas.113.c
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 1 }
    }
}

                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_equipment = 3 } } ITA = { transfer_units_fraction = { target = GRE stockpile_ratio = 0.50 size = 0 } } }

                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_guarantees = 1 } } every_country = { limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA } give_guarantee = GRE } set_global_flag = german_insurances_over_greece }

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Metaxas Ribbentrop Pact Reply Event
	id = hellas.118
	title = {
        text = hellas.118_accepted.t
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    title = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected.t
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_accepted.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected1.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps < 2 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected2.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps = 2 } }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_metaxas_hitler
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
         ###[Calculate Success or Failure]###
            set_temp_variable = { multpl = 100 }                                            ### [Logic] 
            divide_temp_variable = { multpl = GRE.mr_negotiations_threshold }                 # Since the threshold is reduced based of inf/axal, we need to adjust the total rating to 100.
            set_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = GRE.mr_total_ratings }                     # Then we adjust the probabilities. Every point above 50 counts as 2. If we have >95, its 100%.
            multiply_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = multpl }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 50 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 2 }
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = adjusted_total
                min = 0
                max = 100
            }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { adjusted_total > 94.99 } } set_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 100 } }
            round_temp_variable = adjusted_total
            set_temp_variable = { cnter_chance = 100 }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { cnter_chance = adjusted_total }
            random_list = {
                log = yes
                seed = random
                var:adjusted_total = { set_temp_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
                var:cnter_chance = { set_temp_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
            }
         ###[Success Effects]###
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
                ###[Green Light for Naval Invasion]###
                GER = { set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes } }
                set_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact
            }
        }
    }

	option = {
		name = hellas.118.a
        effect_tooltip = {
            GER = { set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes } }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = mr_no_declaration_tt
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.118.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps < 2 } }
        add_to_variable = { mr_total_attemps = 1 }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.117 days = 0 } } }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.118.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
    }
}

            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_arsl_selected = 3 } } set_variable = { mrlim_arsl = 400 } }

            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_better_tariffs = 1 } } add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_cheaper_trade_to_GER days = 720 } GER = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GER_cheaper_trade_to_GRE days = 720 } } }

            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_mineral_athens = 1 } } 
                GRE = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 47 } }

                    set_variable = { return_owner = GER.id }

                }

            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_work_force = 1 } } GRE = { add_timed_idea =  { idea = GRE_work_force_in_Germany_low_GRE days = 180 } } GER = { add_timed_idea =  { idea = GRE_work_force_in_Germany_low_GER days = 180 } } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_work_force = 2 } } GRE = { add_timed_idea =  { idea = GRE_work_force_in_Germany_med_GRE days = 180 } } GER = { add_timed_idea =  { idea = GRE_work_force_in_Germany_med_GER days = 180 } } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_work_force = 3 } } GRE = { add_timed_idea =  { idea = GRE_work_force_in_Germany_high_GRE days = 180 } } GER = { add_timed_idea =  { idea = GRE_work_force_in_Germany_high_GER days = 180 } } }
            ###[Political Arrangements]###
            ##[Land Acquisition]##
            if = { limit = { ENG = { controls_state = 164 } check_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE > 59 } } transfer_state = 164 } else = { transfer_state = 164 }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 44 transfer_state = 805 transfer_state = 115 transfer_state = 156 }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_greek_land_acq = 1 } } GRE = { transfer_state = 117 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_greek_land_acq = 2 } } GRE = { transfer_state = 117 transfer_state = 2 transfer_state = 157 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_greek_land_acq = 3 } } GRE = { transfer_state = 117 transfer_state = 2 transfer_state = 157 transfer_state = 114 transfer_state = 163 transfer_state = 162 } }
            ##[North Africa]##
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_north_afr_aff = 1 } } 
                every_state = {
                    limit = { 
                        OR = { is_owned_by = ITA is_controlled_by = ITA }
                        OR = { is_on_continent = africa is_on_continent = middle_east }
                    }
                    if = { limit = { is_owned_by = ITA } GER = { set_state_owner = PREV } }
                    if = { limit = { is_controlled_by = ITA } GER = { set_state_controller = PREV } }
                }
            }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_north_afr_aff = 2 } } 
                every_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = { is_owned_by = ITA is_controlled_by = ITA }
                        OR = { is_on_continent = africa is_on_continent = middle_east }
                    }
                    if = { limit = { is_owned_by = ITA NOT = { is_core_of = LBA } } GER = { set_state_owner = PREV } }
                    if = { limit = { is_controlled_by = ITA NOT = { is_core_of = LBA } } GER = { set_state_controller = PREV } }
                    if = { limit = { is_core_of = LBA } GRE = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                }
                release_puppet_on_controlled = LBA
            }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_north_afr_aff = 3 } } 
                every_state = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = { is_owned_by = ITA is_controlled_by = ITA }
                        OR = { is_on_continent = africa is_on_continent = middle_east }
                    }
                    if = { 
                        limit = { 
                            OR = { is_owned_by = ITA is_controlled_by = ITA } 
                            OR = { is_core_of = EGY is_owned_by = ENG is_owned_by = FRA } 
                        } 
                        if = { limit = { is_owned_by = ITA } GER = { set_state_owner = PREV } }
                        if = { limit = { is_controlled_by = ITA } GER = { set_state_controller = PREV } }
                    }
                    else_if = { 
                        limit = { 
                            OR = { is_controlled_by = ITA is_owned_by = ITA } 
                            NOT = { is_owned_by = ENG is_owned_by = FRA is_core_of = EGY } 
                        } 
                        GRE = { transfer_state = PREV } 
                    }
                }
                release_puppet_on_controlled = LBA
                release_puppet_on_controlled = ETH
                release_puppet_on_controlled = ERI
                release_puppet_on_controlled = SOM
            }
            ##[Northern Italian State]##
            ITA = { set_capital = { state = 159 } }
            ITA = { white_peace = ENG white_peace = GRE }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_ital_north = 1 } } GER = { puppet = ITA } ITA = { set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality } } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_ital_north = 2 } } ITA = { leave_faction = yes set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality } set_rule = { can_join_factions = no can_create_factions = no can_not_declare_war = yes can_send_volunteers = no } } GRE = { give_guarantee = ITA } GER = { give_guarantee = ITA } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_ital_north = 3 } } GRE = { puppet = ITA } ITA = { leave_faction = yes set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality } } }
            ##[Mussolini's Fate]##
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_mussolini_fate = 1 } } 
                add_political_power = -200 
                every_state = {
                    limit = { 
                        is_controlled_by = GRE
                        is_core_of = ITA
                    }
                    add_resistance = 15
                }
            }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_mussolini_fate = 2 } } 
                every_state = {
                    limit = { 
                        is_controlled_by = GRE
                        is_core_of = ITA
                    }
                    add_compliance = 15
                }
            }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_mussolini_fate = 3 } } 
                add_political_power = 300 
                every_state = {
                    limit = { 
                        is_controlled_by = GRE
                        is_core_of = ITA
                    }
                    add_compliance = 10
                }
            }
            ##[Border Limitations]##
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_demil_selected = 1 } } 
                every_state = {
                    limit = { 
                        NOT = { is_core_of = GRE } 
                        is_on_continent = europe
                        THIS.controller = { 
                            OR = {
                                tag = GRE
                                is_in_faction_with = GRE 
                                is_puppet_of = GRE
                                is_subject_of = GRE
                            }
                        } 
                    }
                    every_neighbor_state = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                is_controlled_by = GER
                                THIS.controller = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
                            }
                        }
                        PREV = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
                        add_to_variable = { GRE.mr_demil_selected_states = 1 }
                    }
                }
            }
            ###################[Basic Stuff]######################
            set_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_war
            set_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_big_war
            GER = { set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = no } }
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GER
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            }
            add_stability = 0.5
            add_war_support = 0.5
            news_event = { id = hellenic_news.154 }
            if = { limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_army } } country_event = { id = hellas.798 } }
            if = { limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_army_reform_hellenic_staff } } country_event = { id = hellas.799 } }
            complete_national_focus = GRE_the_weaves_of_fate
            set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
            clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = hellas.119.a
        clr_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact
        set_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact_Concluded
        MR_clear_variables = yes
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### PEACE ACHIEVED
	id = hellas.806
	title = hellas.806.t
	desc = hellas.806.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.806.a
         
        every_country = {
            limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
            white_peace = GRE
        }
        news_event = { id = hellenic_news.154 }
        complete_national_focus = GRE_the_weaves_of_fate
        complete_national_focus = GRE_glorious_struggle_in_triumph
        set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
        clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        if = { 
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_all_three_demanded }    
            GRE = { transfer_state = 44 }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }    
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_two_demanded }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }  
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_ne_demanded }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_dod_demanded }  
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }  
        }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_stockpile_and_units_disbanded }    
            BUL = { 
                #teleport_armies = { to_state = 48 } 
                delete_unit = {
                    state = 48
                    disband = yes
                }
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 1
                    stockpile_ratio = 1
                    army_ratio = 1
                    navy_ratio = 1
                    air_ratio = 1
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_stockpile }
            BUL = {
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 1
                    stockpile_ratio = 1
                    army_ratio = 0
                    navy_ratio = 0
                    air_ratio = 0
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_units_disbanded }
            BUL = { 
                #teleport_armies = { to_state = 48 } 
                delete_unit = { 
                    state = 48
                    disband = yes
                }
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 0
                    stockpile_ratio = 0.5
                    army_ratio = 0
                    navy_ratio = 0
                    air_ratio = 0
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                   ### Tsouderos                                                                      
	id = hellas.9995
	title = hellas.9995.t
	desc = hellas.9995.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
    
	
	option = {                                                                            
		name = hellas.9995.a
        
        GRE_king_george = { remove_country_leader_role = { ideology = despotism } }
        promote_character = GRE_emmanouil_tsouderos
        if = {
            limit = {

	id = hellas.1003
	title = hellas.1003.t
	desc = hellas.1003.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hellenic_state

	is_triggered_only = yes 
    
	fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_global_flag = weekly_favor_mechanic_frozen
            set_global_flag = GRE_hellenic_state_formed
            set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
            set_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding
            clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
            create_dynamic_country = {
                original_tag = GRE
                save_global_event_target_as = hellenic_state
                #############################[Preliminary State Transfer]############################
                every_state = {
                    limit = {
                        is_owned_by = GRE
                        NOT = { state = 182 }
                    }
                    event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = PREV }
                }
                GER = { transfer_state = 47 transfer_state = 839 }                                                                   # TEMPORARILY TO NAVAL INVADE CRETE (doesn't work otherwise)
                set_capital = { state = 47 }
                add_to_array = { global.axis_occupiers=GER.id }
                add_to_array = { global.axis_occupiers=ITA.id }
                #############################[Setup Occupation Zones]############################
                841 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                731 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                839 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                838 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                47 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                187 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                835 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                836 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                837 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                186 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                185 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                842 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                #######################[Bulgarian Direct Annexations (Historical)]###############
                if = {                                                                                                              # If Bulgaria is alive, in Axis and historical stuff should happen.
                    limit = {
                        BUL = {
                            exists = yes
                            OR = {
                                is_in_faction_with = GER
                                is_in_faction_with = ITA
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    731 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    731 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    731 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    839 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    839 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    839 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    841 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    841 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    841 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    184 = { BUL = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                    840 = { BUL = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                    add_to_array = { global.axis_occupiers=BUL.id }
                }
                else = {
                    184 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }                                      # Italians take control of their portion, as this would have happened historically since the Germans only took strategic regions and Italians the mass of land.
                    840 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                }
                ################################[Set HS Rules]###################################
                set_rule = { 
                    can_join_factions = no 
                    can_create_factions = no
                    can_not_declare_war = yes
                    can_send_volunteers = no
                }
                ################################[Political Setting]###################################
                set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
                set_popularities = { democratic = 15 fascism = 50 neutrality = 20 communism = 15 }
                set_cosmetic_tag = GRE_HELLENIC_STATE_fascism
                GRE = {                                                                     ## Disband Units in Aegean Islands and mainland Greece
                    delete_unit = {state = 835 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 47 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 186 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 187 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 842 disband = yes}
                    set_temp_variable = { convoy_num = GRE.convoys_secured }
                    multiply_temp_variable = { convoy_num = -1 }
                    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                        type = convoy_1
                        amount = convoy_num
                        producer = GRE
                    }
                    transfer_units_fraction = {                                             ## Germany takes 75% of stockpile from virtually SURRENDERED troops
                        target = GER                                                         # This is why evacuated divisions will retain equipment, while disbanded (see above) will put eq to stockpile.
                        size = 0                                                             # So basically the 25% left is what you """evacuated""" to Crete.
                        stockpile_ratio = 0.75
                        army_ratio = 0
                        navy_ratio = 0.0
                        air_ratio = 0.0
                        keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
                    }
                }
                ################################[Characters/Technologies/Ideas/Focuses]###################################
                HS_split_characters_to_respective_nations=yes
                promote_character = GRE_georgios_tsolakoglou
                if = { limit = { GRE = { has_country_flag = archbishop_damaskinos_elected } } event_target:hellenic_state = { complete_national_focus = oust_chrysanthus_for_damaskinos } }
                inherit_technology = GRE
                set_research_slots = 0
                add_ideas = HS_ind_shackles_4
                add_ideas = HS_tripple_occupation
                add_ideas = HS_occupation_costs
                add_ideas = HS_german_plundering
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier=HS_death }
                #add_ideas = HS_death
                if = {
                    limit = { GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } }
                    add_ideas = HS_spirit_of_grand_coalition
                }
                load_focus_tree = hellenic_state_focus
                GRE = { GR_HS_split_ideas = yes }
                #GER = { puppet = event_target:hellenic_state }
                complete_national_focus = glorious_struggle_in_vain
                complete_national_focus = hellenic_state
                complete_national_focus = appoint_tsolakoglou
            }
            every_country = {
                limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = non_aggression_pact
                    active = yes
                }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = military_access
                    active = yes
                }
            }
            GER = {
                add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_german_ambition_crete days = 60 }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = guarantee
                    active = yes
                }
                remove_ideas = GRE_german_ambition
            }
            ITA = {
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = guarantee
                    active = yes
                }
            }
            HS_calculate_initial_anger_level = yes
            HS_set_up_occupation_zones = yes
            HS_set_up_areas_of_interest_arrays = yes
            HS_calculate_factories_in_occupation_zones = yes
            HS_flag_states = yes 
            HS_shut_down_the_games_resistance_mechanic_in_states = yes
            #######[Resource Rights for Sterea/Pel. go to the Reich]######
            ITA = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 835 } }
            ITA = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 186 } }
            ##############################################################
            GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.1004 days = 10 } }
        }
    }
	
	option = { name = hellas.1003.a }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Deploys Andartes
	id = hellas.1600
	title = hellas.1600.t
	desc = hellas.1600.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=0
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { THIS.andartes=th }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=combatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=th }
            add_to_variable = { THIS.available_combatants=tmp }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=noncombatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=th }
            add_to_variable = { THIS.available_noncombatants=tmp }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=reservist_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=th }
            add_to_variable = { THIS.available_reservists=tmp }
            clr_state_flag = state_deploying_recalling
            clear_variable = th
        }
    }

    option = { name=hellas.1600.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Restructures Troops in State
	id = hellas.1602
	title = hellas.1602.t
	desc = hellas.1602.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=1
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ##############
            #[Combatants]#
            ##############
            set_temp_variable={ x=gui_combatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable={ x=THIS.andartes }
            set_variable={ available_combatants=x }
            set_variable={ combatant_percentage=gui_combatant_percentage }
            ##################
            #[Non-Combatants]#
            ##################
            set_temp_variable={ x=gui_noncombatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable={ x=THIS.andartes }
            if = { 
                limit = {                                                                                       # We have enough available non combatants.
                    set_temp_variable={ xx=gui_noncombatant_percentage }
                    multiply_temp_variable={ xx=THIS.andartes }
                    check_variable={ var=xx value=THIS.allocated_noncombatants compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                }
                subtract_from_temp_variable={ x=THIS.allocated_noncombatants }
            }
            else ={ reset_entire_state_unarmed_resistance=yes }                                                 # We do not have enough and need to take from allocated.
            set_variable={ available_noncombatants=x }
            set_variable={ noncombatant_percentage=gui_noncombatant_percentage }
            ##############
            #[Reservists]#
            ##############
            set_temp_variable={ x=gui_reservist_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable={ x=THIS.andartes }
            set_variable={ available_reservists=x }
            set_variable={ reservist_percentage=gui_reservist_percentage }
            clr_state_flag = state_restructuring_forces
        }
    }

    option = { name=hellas.1602.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Adds/Removes Equipment
	id = hellas.1603
	title = hellas.1603.t
	desc = hellas.1603.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=1
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = { has_state_flag = { flag=state_redeploying_equipment value=1 } }
                add_to_variable={ infeq=gui_infeq }
                add_to_variable={ supeq=gui_supeq }
                add_to_variable={ arteq=gui_arteq }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_state_flag = { flag=state_redeploying_equipment value=2 } }
                add_to_variable={ GRE.andartes_infeq_reserve=gui_infeq }
                add_to_variable={ GRE.andartes_supeq_reserve=gui_supeq }
                add_to_variable={ GRE.andartes_arteq_reserve=gui_arteq }
            }
            clear_variable = gui_infeq
            clear_variable = gui_supeq
            clear_variable = gui_arteq
            clr_state_flag = state_redeploying_equipment
        }
    }
    
    option = { name=hellas.1603.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }
}

country_event = {                                                                                
	id = hellas.10000
	title = hellas.10000.t
	desc = {                                                                                        ## Crete did not fall
        text = hellas.10000a.desc
        trigger = {
            GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_holds }
        }
    }
    desc = {                                                                                        ## Crete fell
        text = hellas.10000b.desc
        trigger = {
            GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_falls }
        }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_germany_politician_handshake

	#trigger = {
    #    original_tag = GRE
    #    is_ai = no
    #    date > 1941.06.15
    #    event_target:hellenic_state = { NOT = { controls_state = 47 } }
    #}
    
    timeout_days = 6
    is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            country_event = { id = hellas.10001 days = 7 }
        }
    }
	
	option = {                                                                            
		name = hellas.10000.a
        
        event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 47 }
        event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 839 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 11818 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 4109 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 11965 }
        47 = { add_resistance = 6 }
        if = {
            limit = { GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_falls } }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 270 }
            event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 182 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 12058 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 1164 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 9940 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 4170 }
            add_to_array = { global.greek_occupied_states_all = 182 }
            add_to_array = { global.german_occupied_states = 182 }
            182 = { 
                add_resistance = 9 
                #add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = unyielding_greeks_angered }
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone }
            }
            HS_calculate_factories_in_occupation_zones = yes
            country_event = { id = hellas.1007 days = 0 }
        }
        else = {
            country_event = { id = hellas.1006 days = 0 }
        }
    }
}

	desc = hellas.10001.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_germany_politician_handshake

	fire_only_once = yes
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            HS_shut_down_the_games_resistance_mechanic_in_states=yes

            ###################################

            ###################################
            if = {
                limit = { is_in_array={ array=GRE.occupier_nations value=GER.id }}
                activate_mission=kommandatur
